 Nail polish makes your hands even more beautiful, but when applying nail polish on the nails, if the nail paint is applied in a bad way, then it makes your nails and hands look ugly
 aaie jaane, nail paint lagaate samay dhyaan rakhane vaali ye 6 baaten
 
 
 1
 nail paintalgate samay dhyaan rakhen ki jab aapke nakhun puri tarah sookhe hon, tab hi nail paint lagaaein
 Do not forget to shave your nails before applying nail paint
 2
 After giving the nails a good and perfect shape, first apply a transparent base coat of nail paint, start applying the transparent nail paint between the nails with a brush and once again dip the brush in transparent nail paint and brush it into two separate parts of the nails
 Also apply one coat each
 3
 Transparent nail paint base coat dries well then after that take the nail paint color of your choice and apply the way the transparent nail paint base coat is on the nails
 usee tarah apane pasandida nail polish ke rang ko bhi nakhunon par base kot ke upar lagaaein
 If the color looks light, then after the first coat is dry, apply a second coat of nail polish color
 4
 Always apply a good nail polish, if your nail polish is not good then after applying the nail polish, soak your fingers in ice water, this will set the nail polish on your nails well and shine
 5
 If your nail polish has started on the outside edges of the nails, clean it carefully and thoroughly with the nail polish remover so that the nail polish on your nails looks nice and clean
 6
 After applying nail polish on the nails, soak your hands in cold water, this will make your nail polish more solid as well as look clean, do any work only after the nail polish is completely dry
